<t>CREATE TABLE quantum_computing_research (
    research_id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    researcher_name VARCHAR(50),
    research_topic VARCHAR(100),
    publish_date DATE
);

CREATE TABLE quantum_computing_results (
    result_id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    research_id INT REFERENCES quantum_computing_research(research_id),
    result_description TEXT,
    result_date DATE
